#### ENGLISH PRE-ECW FACTION EVENTS ###

country_event = {
	id = ENG_ForShip.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ENG_ForShip.1" }
	title = ENG_ForShip.1.t
	desc = ENG_ForShip.1.desc
	hidden = yes
	#picture = GFX_report_event_lithuania_army

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ENG_ForShip.1.a
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			set_variable = { TNO_Britain_ElectionSeason_AP_v = -5 }
			set_variable = { TNO_Britain_ElectionSeason_AP_pi = 14 }
		   TNO_Britain_ElectionSeason_AddPop_InState = yes
		   custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_ParliamentMechanic_Party_Support_14_add
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ENG_Player_HMMLR
			country_event = { id = ENG_ForShip.3 days = 15 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ENG_ForShip.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ENG_ForShip.3" }
	title = ENG_ForShip.3.t
	desc = ENG_ForShip.3.desc
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ENG_ForShip.3.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = ENG_Player_HMMLR }
		randomize_temp_variable = {
			var = debuff
			distribution = binomial
			min = 7
			max = 10
		}
		set_variable = { ENG_OFN_Relations_Debuff = debuff }
		round_variable = ENG_OFN_Relations_Debuff
		subtract_from_variable = { ENG_OFN_Relations = ENG_OFN_Relations_Debuff }
		ENG_SE_ClampOFNRelations = yes
		country_event = { id = ENG_ForShip.3 days = 15 }
	}

	option = {
		name = ENG_ForShip.3.b
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ENG_Player_HMMLR } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ENG_ForShip.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ENG_ForShip.4" }
	title = ENG_ForShip.4.t
	desc = ENG_ForShip.4.desc
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ENG_ForShip.4.a
		add_to_variable = { ENG_OFN_Relations = 10 }
		ENG_SE_ClampOFNRelations = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ENG_HMMLR_Speakers_5
			}
			clr_country_flag = ENG_HMMLR_Speakers_5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ENG_HMMLR_Speakers_4
			}
			clr_country_flag = ENG_HMMLR_Speakers_4
			set_country_flag = ENG_HMMLR_Speakers_5
			country_event = { id = ENG_ForShip.4 days = 15 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ENG_HMMLR_Speakers_3
			}
			clr_country_flag = ENG_HMMLR_Speakers_3
			set_country_flag = ENG_HMMLR_Speakers_4
			country_event = { id = ENG_ForShip.4 days = 15 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ENG_HMMLR_Speakers_2
			}
			clr_country_flag = ENG_HMMLR_Speakers_2
			set_country_flag = ENG_HMMLR_Speakers_3
			country_event = { id = ENG_ForShip.4 days = 15 }
		}
		else = {
			clr_country_flag = ENG_HMMLR_Speakers_1
			set_country_flag = ENG_HMMLR_Speakers_2
			country_event = { id = ENG_ForShip.4 days = 15 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #HMMLR asks USA for enough equipment and spares for a tank div
	id = ENG_ForShip.6
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ENG_ForShip.6" }
	title = ENG_ForShip.6.t
	desc = ENG_ForShip.6.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_lend_lease

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #USA approves
		name = ENG_ForShip.6.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = -492 producer = USA }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = APC_equipment amount = -240 producer = USA }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = MBT_equipment amount = -492 producer = USA }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment amount = -29 producer = USA }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment amount = -66 producer = USA }
		hidden_effect = {
			ENG = {
				country_event = { id = ENG_ForShip.7 days = 10 }
				set_country_flag = Hmmlr_special_shipments_approved
				set_country_flag = Hmmlr_special_shipment_1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #USA ain't a fan of the idea
		name = ENG_ForShip.6.b
		hidden_effect = {
			ENG = {
				country_event = { id = ENG_ForShip.7 days = 10 }
				set_country_flag = Hmmlr_special_shipment_1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #HMMLR hears back from the USA
	id = ENG_ForShip.7
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ENG_ForShip.7" }
	title = {
		text = ENG_ForShip.7.t_approved
		trigger = { has_country_flag = Hmmlr_special_shipments_approved }
	}
	title = {
		text = ENG_ForShip.7.t_denied
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Hmmlr_special_shipments_approved } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ENG_ForShip.7.desc_approved
		trigger = { has_country_flag = Hmmlr_special_shipments_approved }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ENG_ForShip.7.desc_denied
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Hmmlr_special_shipments_approved } }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_lend_lease

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #USA approved
		name = ENG_ForShip.7.a
		trigger = { has_country_flag = Hmmlr_special_shipments_approved }
		hidden_effect = {
			ENG = {
				set_country_flag = Hmmlr_guns_special
				ENG_SE_Hmmlr_Guns = yes
				clr_country_flag = Hmmlr_guns_shipment_ongoing
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #USA wasn't a fan of the idea
		name = ENG_ForShip.7.b
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = Hmmlr_special_shipments_approved } }
		hidden_effect = {
			ENG = {
				clr_country_flag = Hmmlr_guns_shipment_ongoing
			}
		}
	}
}

		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = ENG_Player_Collab } }

#### ENGLISH ECONOMY ###

country_event = {
	id = ENG_Econ.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ENG_Econ.1" }
	title = ENG_Econ.1.t
	desc = ENG_Econ.1.desc
	#picture = GFX_report_event_lithuania_army
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = ENG_Econ.1.a

		### ENGLISH ECONOMY SYSTEM INITALIZATION ###
		set_variable = { working_pop = 0.8 }
		set_variable = { industrial_expertise_GDP_bonus = 0.27 }
		set_variable = { industrial_equipment_GDP_bonus = 0.21 }
		set_variable = { education_GDP_bonus = 0.25 }
		set_variable = { research_GDP_bonus = 0.27 }
		set_variable = { dev_tech_GDP_bonus = 1 }
		# These are required temp var for ENG_SE_GDPUpdate due to check_variable issues
		set_variable = { workPop_temp = 0 }
		set_variable = { econ_temp_var = 0 }

		every_owned_state = {
			add_to_variable = { ROOT.econ_temp_var = state_population_k }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			#Get the total working population
			set_temp_variable = { workPop = state_population_k } #pop in the thousands
			multiply_temp_variable = { workPop = ROOT.working_pop }

			#Getting unemployment of 20-25%
			randomize_temp_variable = {
				var = unemploymentTemp
				distribution = uniform
				min = 20
				max = 25
			}
			set_variable = { unemployment = unemploymentTemp }
			divide_variable = { unemployment = 100 }

			#Setting up the job distribution such that 5-10% of all jobs are foreign jobs
			randomize_temp_variable = {
				var = job_ratio
				distribution = uniform
				min = 90
				max = 95
			}
			set_variable = { domestic_business_ratio = job_ratio }
			divide_variable = { domestic_business_ratio = 100 }

			#Get the amount of employed working population
			set_temp_variable = { employPop = 1 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { employPop = unemployment }
			multiply_variable = { employPop = workPop }

			#Set the number of domestic and foreign jobs
			set_variable = { domestic_jobs = employPop }
			multiply_variable = { domestic_jobs = domestic_business_ratio }
			multiply_variable = { domestic_jobs = state_population_k }
			multiply_variable = { domestic_jobs = ROOT.working_pop }
			set_variable = { foreign_jobs = 1 }
			subtract_from_variable = { foreign_jobs = domestic_business_ratio }
			multiply_variable = { foreign_jobs = employPop }
			multiply_variable = { foreign_jobs = state_population_k }
			multiply_variable = { foreign_jobs = ROOT.working_pop }

			#Filler values below
			set_variable = { domestic_job_growth = 0.001 }
			set_variable = { foreign_job_growth = 0.001 }

			#Calculate state GDP relative to population
			set_temp_variable = { state_GDP_temp = state_population_k }
			divide_temp_variable = { state_GDP_temp = ROOT.econ_temp_var }
			multiply_temp_variable = { state_GDP_temp = ROOT.GDP }
			set_variable = { state_GDP = state_GDP_temp } #in millions
			#Change existing TNO state GDP to match
			set_variable = { state_value = state_GDP }

			#Assuming domestic/foreign GDP value is same for now
			#Thus divide state GDP by employed pop to get value
			set_temp_variable = { total_jobs = domestic_jobs }
			add_to_temp_variable = { total_jobs = foreign_jobs }
			set_variable = { domestic_GDP_value = state_GDP } #in millions per 1000 jobs
			divide_variable = { domestic_GDP_value = total_jobs }
			set_variable = { foreign_GDP_value = domestic_GDP_value } #in millions per 1000 jobs

			#Get GDP per capita
			set_variable = { GDP_per_capita = state_GDP }
			divide_variable = { GDP_per_capita = workPop }
			multiply_variable = { GDP_per_capita = 1000 }	#in millions; multiply as workPop is in thousands
			round_variable = GDP_per_capita
		}
		set_country_flag = ENG_CF_EnglishEconomy
	}
}

		1300 = { ENG_SE_DecreaseForeignJobGrowth_0.01 = yes }
		1300 = { ENG_SE_DecreaseForeignJobGrowth_0.01 = yes }
		1300 = { ENG_SE_DecreaseForeignJobGrowth_0.01 = yes }
	}

	id = ENG_intro.1

country_event = { #The king's safety ticker
	id = ENG_intro.13
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ENG_intro.13"
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = ENG_FutureSpeechSafetyMeter
			}
			add_to_variable = { ENG_FutureSpeechSafetyMeter = ENG_FutureSpeechSafetyMeter_Periodic }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = ENG_the_prime_minister_speaks
				}
				add_to_variable = { ENG_FutureSpeechSafetyMeter_Periodic = -1 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = ENG_the_prime_minister_speaks
				}
				add_to_variable = { ENG_FutureSpeechSafetyMeter_Periodic = 1 }
			}
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					country_event = { id = ENG_intro.13 days = 4 }
				}
				50 = {
					country_event = { id = ENG_intro.13 days = 6 }
				}
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = ENG_FutureSpeechSafetyMeter_Periodic
				min = -10
				max = 10
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = ENG_FutureSpeechSafetyMeter
				min = 0
				max = 100
			}
		}
	}
	title = ENG_intro.13.t
	desc = ENG_intro.13.desc
	#picture =

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = no
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		name = ENG_intro.13.a
	}
}

					days = 25

					id = ENG_flavor.46
					days = 80
				}
			}
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.50003
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ENG_thatcher.1028" }
	title = ENG_thatcher.1028.t
	desc = ENG_thatcher.1028.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_westminister

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #
		name = ENG_thatcher.1028.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = ENG_thatcher_slow_monetarism4
			add_idea = ENG_thatcher_slow_monetarism5
		}
		every_owned_state = { ENG_SE_IncreaseDomesticJobsValue_Massive = yes }
		every_owned_state = { ENG_SE_IncreaseForeignJobsValue_Massive = yes }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ENG_thatcher.1029
				days = 365
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_monetarism_poverty_decrease.tt
	}
}

	}

	option = { #
		name = ENG_Wales_unification.1.a

country_event = { #sending message to wales asking for reunification
	id = ENG_Wales_unification.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ENG_Wales_unification.2" }
	title = ENG_Wales_unification.2.t
	desc = ENG_Wales_unification.2.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_iberia_guy_paper_meeting

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #yes
		name = ENG_Wales_unification.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1

			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				WAL = { has_government = despotism }
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				ENG = { has_government = social_conservative }
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				ENG = { has_government = socialist }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = ENG_WALES_REUNIFICATION
					option = ENG_WALES_REUNIFICATION_WAR
				}
			}
		}
		ENG = {
			country_event = {
				id = ENG_Wales_unification.3
				days = 1
			}
		}
		WAL = {
			country_event = {
				id = ENG_Wales_unification.4
				days = 1
			}
		}

	}
	option = { #no
		name = ENG_Wales_unification.2.b
		ai_chance = { 
		    factor = 2 
		    modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = ENG_WALES_REUNIFICATION
					option = ENG_WALES_REUNIFICATION_PEACEFUL
				}
			}
		}
		ENG = {
			country_event = {
				id = ENG_Wales_unification.17
				days = 1
			}
		}

	}
}

country_event = { #england asks for demilitirisation
	id = ENG_Wales_unification.5
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ENG_Wales_unification.5" }
	title = ENG_Wales_unification.5.t
	desc = ENG_Wales_unification.5.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_iberia_meeting_small

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #yes
		name = ENG_Wales_unification.5.a
		ai_chance = { 
		    factor = 1 
		    modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = ENG_WALES_REUNIFICATION
					option = ENG_WALES_REUNIFICATION_WAR
				}
			}
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment amount = -600 producer = WAL }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment amount = -150 producer = WAL }
		ENG = {
			country_event = {
				id = ENG_Wales_unification.6
				days = 1
			}
		}

	}
	option = { #no
		name = ENG_Wales_unification.5.b
		ai_chance = { 
		    factor = 1 
		    modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = ENG_WALES_REUNIFICATION
					option = ENG_WALES_REUNIFICATION_PEACEFUL
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_Wales_Collab_War_tt
		ENG = {
			country_event = {
				id = ENG_Wales_unification.14
				days = 1
			}
		}

	}
}

country_event = { #Welsh Terrorism - exists/
	id = ENG_Wales_unification.16
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ENG_Wales_unification.16" }
	title = ENG_Wales_unification.16.t
	desc = {
		text = ENG_Wales_unification.16.desc
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = ENG_Wales_Violent
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ENG_Wales_unification.166.desc
			trigger = {
				has_idea = ENG_Wales_Resistance
			}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ENG_Wales_unification.1666.desc
			trigger = {
				has_idea = ENG_Wales_Riots
			}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ENG_Wales_unification.16666.desc
			trigger = {
				has_idea = ENG_Wales_Protests
			}
	}
	desc = {
		text = ENG_Wales_unification.166666.desc
			trigger = {
				has_idea = ENG_Wales_Civil_Unrest
			}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_terrorist_attack

	is_triggered_only = yes
	#fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #yes
		name = ENG_Wales_unification.16.a
		ENG_Decrease_Welsh_Terrorism = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = ENG_Wales_Riots
				322 = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = ENG
					}
				}
			}
			add_state_core = 1301
			add_state_core = 122
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #NDL 1st Election Victory
	id = ENG_Government_Changes.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ENG_Government_Changes.1" }
	title = ENG_Government_Changes.1.t
	desc = ENG_Government_Changes.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_eng_jellicoe

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes 
	
	option = {
		name = ENG_Government_Changes.1.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ENG_flavor.39
				days = 5
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = ENG_HMMLR_Post_Reconstruction_Conservative
				name = ENG_HMMLR_Post_Reconstruction_Conservative_long
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Enoch Powell"
				desc = "POLITICS_ENOCH_POWELL_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_Enoch_Powell.dds"
				expire = "1990.1.1"
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Harold Wilson"
				desc = "POLITICS_HAROLD_WILSON_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_England_Harold_Wilson_60s.dds"
				expire = "1990.1.1"
				ideology = socialist_subtype
				traits = { }
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_conservative
			}

			### Paaaaarliament mechanic stuff
				# NOTE: Because of how arrays start at zero, the ID's for each party here are one less than normal
				# So instead of 8 being the Royal Party, it would be the National Front
				## Party Support
				# National Democratic League
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_Support^10 = 0.56 } # NDL New Whigs
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_Support^11 = 0.73 } # NDL Democrats
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_Support^12 = 0.48 } # NDL Patriots
				# Socialist Labour Party
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_Support^13 = 0.32 } # SLP Progress
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_Support^14 = 0.13 } # SLP Pollitites
				# Movement in Support of the Army
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_Support^15 = 0.14 } # MSA
	
				## Party Government Status
				# National Democratic League
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_GovStatus^10 = 2 } # NDL New Whigs  (Governing)
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_GovStatus^11 = 1 } # NDL Democrats  (Leading)
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_GovStatus^12 = 2 } # NDL Patriots   (Governing)
				# Socialist Labour Party
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_GovStatus^13 = 3 } # SLP Progress   (Opposition)
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_GovStatus^14 = 3 } # SLP Pollitites (Opposition)
				# Movement in Support of the Army
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_GovStatus^15 = 3 } # MSA			  (Opposition)
	
				## Talking Heads
				ParliamentMechanic_Clean_TalkingHeads = yes
				add_ideas = {
					TNO_ParliamentMechanic_Speaker_George_Jellicoe
					TNO_ParliamentMechanic_Monarch_NoMonarch
					TNO_ParliamentMechanic_OppLeader_Harold_Wilson
				}

				# Wilson's Military effect
				add_to_variable = { ENG_MIL_LOY = 5 }

				## Gov. Stability calculation
				ParliamentMechanic_GovStab_Calculate = yes
			### Paaaaarliament mechanic stuff
	
			load_focus_tree = FEN_FT_NDL_Megatree
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				ENG_David_Eccles_hog
				ENG_Shirley_Williams_eco
			}
			set_country_flag = NDL_victorious
			set_country_flag = ENG_government_monarchy
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			country_event = { id = ENG_diplomatic_crisis.17 days = 360 } #England applies for OFN membership
			country_event = { id = ENG_diplomatic_crisis.9 days = 900 } #Welsh Diplomatic Crisis - 2.5 years after election
			country_event = { id = ENG_diplomatic_crisis.10 days = 1400 } #Scottish Diplomatic Crisis - 4 years after election
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.60002
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Thatcher 1st Election Victory
	id = ENG_Government_Changes.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ENG_Government_Changes.3" }
	title = ENG_Government_Changes.3.t
	desc = ENG_Government_Changes.3.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_eng_thatcher_speech

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes 
	
	option = {
		name = ENG_Government_Changes.3.a
		hidden_effect = {
			kill_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Margaret Thatcher"
				desc = "POLITICS_MARGARET_THATCHER_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_England_Margaret_Thatcher_60s.dds"
				expire = "1990.1.1"
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				traits = { }
			}
			RP_POP_SPLIT_CALC = yes
			RP_ELITE_SPLIT_CALC = yes
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			}

			### Paaaaarliament mechanic stuff
				# NOTE: Because of how arrays start at zero, the ID's for each party here are one less than normal
				# So instead of 8 being the Royal Party, it would be the National Front
				## Party Support
				# Royal Party
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_Support^7 = 0.67 } # Royal Party
				# United England
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_Support^5 = 0.31 } # UE Macmillanists
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_Support^6 = 0.24 } # UE Liberals
				# National Front
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_Support^8 = 0.18 } # National Front

				## Party Government Status
				# Royal Party
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_GovStatus^7 = 1 } # Royal Party	   (Leading)
				# United England
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_GovStatus^5 = 3 } # UE Macmillanists (Opposition)
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_GovStatus^6 = 3 } # UE Liberals	   (Opposition)
				# National Front
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_GovStatus^8 = 3 } # National Front   (Opposition)
	
				## Talking Heads
				ParliamentMechanic_Clean_TalkingHeads = yes
				add_ideas = {
					TNO_ParliamentMechanic_Speaker_Margaret_Thatcher
					TNO_ParliamentMechanic_Monarch_Edward_VIII
					TNO_ParliamentMechanic_OppLeader_Harold_Macmillan
				}

				# Thatcher's Military effect
				add_to_variable = { ENG_MIL_LOY = 5 }

				## Gov. Stability calculation
				ParliamentMechanic_GovStab_Calculate = yes
			### Paaaaarliament mechanic stuff
			
			load_focus_tree = ENG_Thatcher_Megatree
			remove_all_ministers = yes 
			add_ideas = {
				ENG_Rab_Butler_hog
				ENG_John_Biffen_eco
				ENG_Francis_Pym_for
				ENG_Anthony_Barber_sec
			}
			set_country_flag = ENG_Thatcher_victorious
			set_country_flag = ENG_government_monarchy
			#drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			ENG_SE_ThatcherSetVariables = yes
			country_event = { id = ENG_mac.1004 days = 750 } #King Edward announces abdication
			country_event = { id = ENG_diplomatic_crisis.13 days = 900 } #Welsh Diplomatic Crisis - 2.5 years after election
			country_event = { id = ENG_diplomatic_crisis.14 days = 1400 } #Scottish Diplomatic Crisis - 4 years after election
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = WORLD.50014
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = ENG_government_monarchy }
					add_ideas = TNO_ParliamentMechanic_Monarch_Elizabeth_II
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = ENG_government_republic }
					add_ideas = TNO_ParliamentMechanic_Monarch_NoMonarch
				}

				# Jellicoe's Military effect
				add_to_variable = { ENG_MIL_LOY = -5 }
				add_to_variable = { ENG_MIL_EFF = -5 }

				## Gov. Stability calculation
				ParliamentMechanic_GovStab_Calculate = yes
			### Paaaaarliament mechanic stuff

			load_focus_tree = ENG_blankfocus
			remove_all_ministers = yes 
			add_ideas = {
				ENG_Reg_Birch_hog
				ENG_Alfred_Robens_eco
				ENG_Peter_Shore_for
				ENG_Bill_Alexander_sec
			}
			set_country_flag = SLP_victorious2
			set_country_flag = TNO_closing_screen_show
		}
	}
}

	id = ENG_Government_Changes.12
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ENG_Government_Changes.12" }
	title = ENG_Government_Changes.12.t
	desc = ENG_Government_Changes.12.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_ENG_intro_12

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes 
	
	option = {
		name = ENG_Government_Changes.12.a
		hidden_effect = {
			kill_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Margaret Thatcher"
				desc = "POLITICS_MARGARET_THATCHER_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_England_Margaret_Thatcher_70s.dds"
				expire = "1990.1.1"
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				traits = { }
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			}

			### Paaaaarliament mechanic stuff
				# NOTE: Because of how arrays start at zero, the ID's for each party here are one less than normal
				# So instead of 8 being the Royal Party, it would be the National Front
				## Party Support
				# Royal Party
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_Support^7 = 0.67 } # Royal Party
				# United England
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_Support^5 = 0.31 } # UE Macmillanists
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_Support^6 = 0.24 } # UE Liberals
				# National Front
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_Support^8 = 0.18 } # National Front

				## Party Government Status
				# Royal Party
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_GovStatus^7 = 1 } # Royal Party	   (Leading)
				# United England
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_GovStatus^5 = 3 } # UE Macmillanists (Opposition)
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_GovStatus^6 = 3 } # UE Liberals	   (Opposition)
				# National Front
				set_variable = { ParliamentMechanic_Party_GovStatus^8 = 3 } # National Front   (Opposition)
	
				## Talking Heads
				ParliamentMechanic_Clean_Speaker = yes
				ParliamentMechanic_Clean_OppositionLeader = yes
				add_ideas = {
					TNO_ParliamentMechanic_Speaker_Margaret_Thatcher
					TNO_ParliamentMechanic_OppLeader_Harold_Macmillan
				}

				# Thatcher's Military effect
				add_to_variable = { ENG_MIL_LOY = 5 }

				## Gov. Stability calculation
				ParliamentMechanic_GovStab_Calculate = yes
			### Paaaaarliament mechanic stuff

			load_focus_tree = { 
				tree = ENG_thatcher_2
				keep_completed = yes
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes 
			add_ideas = {
				ENG_Keith_Joseph_hog
				ENG_Peter_Thorneycroft_eco
				ENG_Francis_Pym_for
				ENG_Anthony_Barber_sec
			}
			set_country_flag = ENG_Thatcher_victorious2
			set_country_flag = TNO_closing_screen_show
		}
	}
}

#Beginning of Demand
country_event = {
	id = ENG_Cornwall.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] event ENG_Cornwall.3"}
	title = ENG_Cornwall.3.t
	desc = ENG_Cornwall.3.d
	#picture =
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = ENG_Cornwall.3.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { cornwall_started_demand = 6 }
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				add_idea = ENG_Across_The_Channel2
				remove_idea = ENG_Across_The_Channel
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				activate_mission = demand_german_training
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { cornwall_started_demand = 1 }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { cornwall_demand_swap = 0 } }
					set_variable = { cornwall_demand_swap = 1 }
					random_list = {
						30 = {
							activate_mission = demand_german_officers
							set_country_flag = demand_german_officers
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								has_country_flag = demand_german_officers
							}
						}
						30 = {
							activate_mission = demand_german_influence
							set_country_flag = demand_german_influence
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								has_country_flag = demand_german_influence
							}
						}
						30 = {
							activate_mission = demand_german_propaganda
							set_country_flag = demand_german_propaganda
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								has_country_flag = demand_german_propaganda
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					set_variable = { cornwall_demand_swap = 0 }
					random_list = {
						30 = {
							activate_mission = demand_more_guns
							set_country_flag = demand_more_guns
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								has_country_flag = demand_more_guns
							}
						}
						30 = {
							activate_mission = demand_more_artillery
							set_country_flag = demand_more_artillery
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								has_country_flag = demand_more_artillery
							}
						}
						30 = {
							activate_mission = demand_more_motorized
							set_country_flag = demand_more_motorized
							modifier = {
								factor = 0
								has_country_flag = demand_more_motorized
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
